<h1 class="devsite-page-title" style="width:50%" id="compose-material" data-text="Compose Material " tabindex="-1">Compose Material </h1>




  



  
  



  
  








<div style="align:right; text-align:right; padding-bottom:21px; margin-top:-45px; border-bottom:1px solid black;"> 
<a href="/jetpack/compose/tutorial">User Guide</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://github.com/android/compose-samples">Code Sample</a>
</div>



<div style="float:left; font-size:medium; margin-bottom:5px; margin-top:10px" class="nocontent">
<div style="text-align:left; font-size:90%; padding-right:30px; margin-right:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"> 
API Reference<br>

<a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material/package-summary">androidx.compose.material</a><br>
<a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material/icons/package-summary">androidx.compose.material.icons</a><br>
(<em>See the API reference docs for all compose packages</em>)

</div>
</div>

<div style="text-align:left; padding-left:10px; margin-left:10px; margin-top:15px; margin-bottom:10px;">


Build Jetpack Compose UIs with ready to use Material Design Components. This is the higher level entry point of Compose, designed to provide components that match those described at www.material.io.

</div>



<div style="clear:both"></div>









<table style="width:100%">
<tr>
<th style="width:15%">Latest Update</th>
<th style="width:15%">Stable Release</th>
<th style="width:15%">Release Candidate</th>
<th style="width:15%">Beta Release</th>
<th style="width:15%">Alpha Release</th></tr>

<tr>

<td>December 11, 2024</td>


<td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material#1.7.6">1.7.6</a></td>



<td>-</td>




<td>-</td>




<td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material#1.8.0-alpha07">1.8.0-alpha07</a></td>


</tr>
</table>



<h2 id="structure" data-text="Structure" tabindex="-1">Structure</h2>

<p>Compose is combination of 7 Maven Group Ids within <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx</code>.  Each Group
contains a targeted subset of functionality, each with its own set of release
notes.</p>

<p>This table explains the groups and links to each set of release notes.</p>




<table>
  <thead>
    <tr><th>Group</th><th>Description</th></tr>
  </thead>

  <tbody class="list">

    




































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-animation">compose.animation</a></td><td>Build animations in their Jetpack Compose applications to enrich the user experience.</td></tr>

  



    



























































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-compiler">compose.compiler</a></td><td>Transform @Composable functions and enable optimizations with a Kotlin compiler plugin.</td></tr>

  



    


























































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-foundation">compose.foundation</a></td><td>Write Jetpack Compose applications with ready to use building blocks and extend foundation to build your own design system pieces.</td></tr>

  



    




































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material">compose.material</a></td><td>Build Jetpack Compose UIs with ready to use Material Design Components. This is the higher level entry point of Compose, designed to provide components that match those described at www.material.io.</td></tr>

  



    



































































































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-material3">compose.material3</a></td><td>Build Jetpack Compose UIs with Material Design 3 Components, the next evolution of Material Design. Material 3 includes updated theming and components and Material You personalization features like dynamic color, and is designed to be cohesive with the new Android 12 visual style and system UI.</td></tr>

  



    





























































































































































































<tr><td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-runtime">compose.runtime</a></td><td>Fundamental building blocks of Compose's programming model and state management, and core runtime for the Compose Compiler Plugin to target.</td></tr>

<h2 id="declaring_dependencies" data-text="Declaring dependencies" tabindex="-1">Declaring dependencies</h2>

<p>To add a dependency on Compose, you must add the Google Maven repository to your
project. Read <a href="/studio/build/dependencies#google-maven">Google&#39;s Maven repository</a>
for more information.</p>

<p>Add the dependencies for the artifacts you need in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">build.gradle</code> file for
your app or module:</p>














































































































































































































<div>

ideas for improving this library. Please take a look at the
<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues?q=componentid:742043%20status:open">existing issues</a>
in this library before you create a new one. You can add your vote to an existing issue by
clicking the star button.</p>

for more information.</p>

</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Adds support for ripples in expanding components on Android S+, such as a card that expands on click. Previously the ripple would not fill up the new size but now it will expand to the new bounds. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If509acac87caa3f13aa2cf969f7bfade7da3e7f6">If509a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/183019123">b/183019123</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.7.1" data-text="Version 1.7.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.1</h3>

<p>September 10, 2024</p>

<ul>
<li>No changes to Android artifacts. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">-desktop</code> artifacts were removed and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">-jvmStubs</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">-linuxx64Stubs</code> artifacts were added. None of these targets are meant to be used, they are placeholders to help Jetbrains Compose efforts.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0" data-text="Version 1.7.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0</h3>

<p>September 4, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0</code> is released. Version 1.7.0 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d8995e2377dd4baad64b39becb6d480cadd05c86..38ffb9c315c3f894412184bda180c1b58b2a8556/compose/material">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.6.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Material components have been migrated to use the new ripple APIs, and no longer query <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>.</li>
<li>Material components that previously accepted a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> and defaulted to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">remember { MutableInteractionSource() }</code> now accept a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> and default to null instead. If you are not hoisting and using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, you should pass null. This allows for some components to lazily create an instance only when needed, improving performance. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawer</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheet</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackdropScaffold</code> and standard Bottomsheet have been promoted to stable API.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.7.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-beta02</h3>

<p>May 29, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-beta02</code> is released. Version 1.7.0-beta02 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4..1a123f646cfea1599f9efead6da546b0c26063fa/compose/material">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update API for styling the links: moved the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextLinkStyles</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> and removed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> from material (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5477bdb498b6b4f33ab3bc998e2be59d8a4ff7e4">I5477b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.7.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 14, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-beta01</code> is released. Version 1.7.0-beta01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/06bfcd36801b67b9fe9b9bcae0d16a55e7d40fd7..6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4/compose/material">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated the API for getting Material themed links in Text. Specifically, removed the methods from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> for constructing themed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinkAnnotations</code> and parse HTML with themed links. Instead, added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextLinkStyles</code> class that allows to style the links as a parameter to the Text composable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I31b93f4460f4a0a50c7a86996a499d359ba455c8">I31b93</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.7.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>May 1, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-alpha08</code> is released. Version 1.7.0-alpha08 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943..06bfcd36801b67b9fe9b9bcae0d16a55e7d40fd7/compose/material">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix <code translate="no" dir="ltr">backgroundColor</code> not applying to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldDecorationBox</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextFieldDecorationBox</code>. Decoration boxes now accept a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">shape</code> parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I371c26718597cb36ac537e9412ce476532afb40d">I371c2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/307694651">b/307694651</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration#isEnabled</code> has been removed, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalRippleConfiguration</code> has been made nullable. To disable a ripple, instead of providing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isEnabled = false</code>, provide <code translate="no" dir="ltr">null</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalRippleConfiguration</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22725ce120f27f7dd0041bfabff5f3faff614ea9">I22725</a>)</li>
<li>Text links have a pressed state styling option in addition to normal styling, hovered and focused. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDefaults</code> methods each have a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">pressedStyle</code> argument to support that. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic473f81fd32d95ad84d6bc452c8dcbf6de7ba4ba">Ic473f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139312671">b/139312671</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> top padding for label now accounts for system font size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc78176ca566364b041b5863aa477ada660d05a9">Idc781</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.7.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>February 21, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261..e1b82c49c59d8e976ce558aba5586f6c61bc9054/compose/material">Version 1.7.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawer</code> has been promoted from experimental to stable. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code> now exposes the progress as a function, allowing to query progress between specific targets. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code> now allows customizing the animation spec, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmStateChange</code> is not a trailing lambda anymore. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9c029340ea69a755ad0cd8f46b8fcdc76422c41c">I9c029</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261423850">b/261423850</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackdropScaffold</code> has been promoted from experimental to stable. The animation spec is now a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">tween</code> spec in accordance with guidelines. The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snackbarHost</code> parameter of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackdropScaffold</code> is no longer the last parameter to avoid confusion with trailing lambdas. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackdropScaffoldState</code> exposes a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">progress(from, to)</code> API to query progress between anchors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I73f48dd7d1aab0a57d728f562f22bda5020ccd4b">I73f48</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261423218">b/261423218</a>)</li>
<li>Standard bottom sheets have been promoted from experimental to stable. Deprecated constructors have been removed. The animation spec is now a tween spec in accordance with guidelines. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c1a892338d183db35ecf3c023255682b4e785bd">I3c1a8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/278692145">b/278692145</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261409034">b/261409034</a>)</li>
<li>Modal bottom sheets have been promoted from experimental to stable. Deprecated constructors have been removed. The animation spec is now a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">tween</code> spec in accordance with guidelines. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic53f4fe7c7183569cb7322c8f56f571be5316be0">Ic53f4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/278692145">b/278692145</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266780235">b/266780235</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261409034">b/261409034</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackdropScaffold</code> could crash in specific scenarios in combination with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5139666a03c031ae50528e493aa415a9cf00c7d1">I51396</a>)</li>
<li>Removed subcomposition inside <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> to improve performance. Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> would crash in specific scenarios in combination with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2f90cfec6dde3d7c9d351ab3e7d8917b13adb126">I2f90c</a>)</li>
<li>Removed subcomposition inside <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code>, improving performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7a0255c0ad99a0be553f95c13f9fa2eda38b2aeb">I7a025</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.7.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.7.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>February 7, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3abba2d2e4a810f1cf9909ba77546cae2258919d..ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261/compose/material">Version 1.7.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.7.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.7.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.7.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>January 24, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.7.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4c61c4d68d2bf0ccc61e316bc2a03754bb6979cf..3abba2d2e4a810f1cf9909ba77546cae2258919d/compose/material">Version 1.7.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Material components have been migrated to use the new ripple APIs, and no longer query <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code> have been deprecated from material-ripple, with new ripple and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleConfiguration</code> APIs added to material and other design system libraries.</p></li>
<li><p>Material components that previously accepted a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> and defaulted to remember <code translate="no" dir="ltr">{ MutableInteractionSource() }</code> now accept a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> and default to null instead. If you are not hoisting and using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, you should pass null. This allows for some components to lazily create an instance only when needed, improving performance. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components.</p></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>Removed drawer-related functionality from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>. Wrap your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> in a Drawer composable to achieve the previous functionality. See <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffoldWithDrawerSample</code> for an example. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1dcc8c426b3a956c0103c8637b22873c6237b0d9">I1dcc8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Introduced a temporary flag to control whether Scaffold should measure its children during measurement or during placement. By default, this will measure in measurement. If you are facing issues with the new behavior, please file an issue. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If6e3b68c0af4445e5c94f8a49cc64323d7f2ed32">If6e3b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>September 6, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.6.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/216f103fa4a5c7247f7bafc8bb3014616c265f0c..9ce75ea1baa2af10dda8f787f69c40c6654bcac1/compose/material">Version 1.6.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added support for auto-mirrored icons when rendered in right-to-left layouts. Icons in the material-icons-core and material-icons-extended modules are now providing additional icon sets for supporting auto-mirroring when the icon allows it. The new sets are prefixed with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icons.AutoMirrored.Filled...</code> etc., and hold icons that will auto-mirror on RTL layouts. See the <a href="http://developers.google.com/fonts/docs/material_icons">list of Material icons</a> for the list of icons that can (and should) be auto-mirrored.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added support for auto-mirrored icons when rendered in right-to-left layouts. Icons in the material-icons-core and material-icons-extended modules are now providing additional icon sets for supporting auto-mirroring when the icon allows it. The new sets are prefixed with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icons.AutoMirrored.Filled...</code> etc., and hold icons that will auto-mirror on RTL layouts. See the <a href="http://developers.google.com/fonts/docs/material_icons">list of Material icons</a> for the list of icons that can (and should) be auto-mirrored. The previously provided icon properties for those icons are now marked as deprecated, and provides a replacement-block suggestion to help with the migration. In case you don&#39;t have any special handling for mirroring icons on RTL, we recommend migrating to the new set of icons. For example, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icons.Filled.ArrowBack</code> should be refactored to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icons.AutoMirrored.Filled.ArrowBack</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4b5116207cb9c0dd1a8a72d2bd3f606f8fdd0129">I4b511</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>August 23, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.6.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5d7dd999525725bd038a00ca4e89e0fef624a6da..216f103fa4a5c7247f7bafc8bb3014616c265f0c/compose/material">Version 1.6.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where some components using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Subcomposition</code> (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>) inside a Scaffold inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code> were attempting to read their size too early. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If2c5daa98914149d12be03e02ba650c24acf19b8">If2c5d</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">offset</code> calculation so x offsets depend solely on the local layout direction, and y offsets will no longer be reversed when the menu is near the bottom of the screen. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccc743f3306d9b259f0cc21d1089d9479df203fb">Iccc74</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/294103942">b/294103942</a>)</li>
<li>Optimized <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>&#39;s layout internals and fixed a potential issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadLayout</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic0afaf770bc5062ddae0159698402a00cf29bd0c">Ic0afa</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>August 9, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.6.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313..5d7dd999525725bd038a00ca4e89e0fef624a6da/compose/material">Version 1.6.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Material2 components now have a separate API to pass <code translate="no" dir="ltr">windowInsets</code> to support edge-to-edge functionality in android. Unlike material3 components, material2 components do not support insets by default and the value should be passed manually. Refer to the corresponding samples for guidance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I655e87062da5c3b01c3923e6711ba12977e0b3d8">I655e8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.6.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494..4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313/compose/material">Version 1.6.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We are moving the density dependency to the component level. This applies to the following components: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> and Sheet based components. Please use the new overload provided where density is a parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1846ea6aeb659f53eb8bff6895f7aea19af46fe8">I1846e</a>)</li>
<li>Additional annotations to specify allowed inputs to composables (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I51109ce34ab8bb50a8104572d79d2a94b67f3b17">I51109</a>)</li>
<li>Updated API files to annotate compatibility suppression (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e87ae292b38fac1886001f5317acda1592f174b">I8e87a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/287516207">b/287516207</a>)</li>
<li>Added new Start alignment for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FabPosition</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib7aea97d6ac5c6ee33fd10916c74c540ff5889de">Ib7aea</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/170592777">b/170592777</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldColorsWithIcons</code> in Material 2 has been deprecated in favor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldColors</code>. When overriding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">leadingIconColor</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">trailingIconColor</code>, also override the overload with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">interactionSource</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id57eda2be81aa23263a9c9a83e89789934acf169">Id57ed</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/199377790">b/199377790</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>June 21, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.6.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9eb2d144f9209cb9c4205ad1f981eb7ddf29b96e..3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494/compose/material">Version 1.6.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> is now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code> by default in Material 2 typography. The default line height style has also been changed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Trim.None</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Alignment.Center</code>, and explicit <code translate="no" dir="ltr">lineHeight</code> (in sp) have been added to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code>s of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Typography</code>. Consult <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/compose/text/style-paragraph#adjust-line-height">the API docs</a> if you want to customize these values, and see <a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">the blog post</a> for an in-depth explainer of these changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icabc31f64e23ba0b8b92c909a8df1fe5f72ce9ed">Icabc3</a>, <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3f8014ab249694ce695fc7655b6c5d27ca872acd">I3f801</a>, <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I04c0331d11740f21f37b5f480a312012b122d22b">I04c03</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Material&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Swipeable</code> APIs have been deprecated. Please refer to Foundation&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnchoredDraggable</code> APIs which are optimized for both simple and complex use cases. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I732e03d07da57c1231ea2ebd84f793aaab1df2dd">I732e0</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code> now expose a progress property indicating the progress between the current (settled) anchor and the closest anchor in the swipe direction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1b31727b4f56df890e336bea9f4de526733aaacc">I1b317</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/271169225">b/271169225</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/276375124">b/276375124</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/276776071">b/276776071</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/270066861">b/270066861</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p>September 27, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.1</code> is released with no changes. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/65e3f15108d25a7e1c5c841c0855b21eca194070..824a15c9a34e9d13a5f58f4066029f0a784186b6/compose/material">Version 1.5.1 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.5.0" data-text="Version 1.5.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0</h3>

<p>August 9, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d83e1a7d6afe597aed6e48be005010c7a26486dd..65e3f15108d25a7e1c5c841c0855b21eca194070/compose/material">Version 1.5.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.4.0</strong></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable1 APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmStateChange</code> param has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmValueChange</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">progress</code> is now exposed as a float value. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> are internal. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expand()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">collapse()</code> instead. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">direction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">overflow</code> have been removed. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">offset</code> has been replaced with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset()</code>. <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I323b4ebe42e5a3817f27759749d72ad222ac084b">I323b4</a></li>
<li>Mark the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> function in Drawer as non-experimental API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib9c18103d5485a48177a9b57ce40b29656bb4cf1">Ib9c18</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261425368">b/261425368</a>)</li>
<li>Added a track color parameter for circular progress indicators, and a stroke cap parameter for both circular and linear progress indicators. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie668cc47ce9ce3aa688ad3c3ed9e9e15fdbda5e9">Ie668c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/216325962">b/216325962</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222964817">b/222964817</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState.Saver</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberModalBottomSheetState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmStateChange</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmValueChange</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib48d1cbe2671647f5feda1fcde5dee9754c8caa0">Ib48d1</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.minimumInteractiveComponentSize</code>. It can be used to reserve at least 48.dp in size to disambiguate touch interactions if the element would measure smaller. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I33f58e4c11cf74668e97167b91dad26b64ac554b">I33f58</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/258495559">b/258495559</a>)</li>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code>&#39;s animateTo does not take an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animationSpec</code> parameter anymore and the offset exposed is now nullable. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset</code> to require the offset. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia2e79162058b143cc40ab6c4b1082126e147a7a2">Ia2e79</a>)</li>
<li>Adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@JvmDefaultWithCompatibility</code> annotation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8f2067bb0754a5e9dc70c934403366ca8d319c36">I8f206</a>)</li>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalDrawer. DrawerState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> has been replaced by the open and close methods and the offset is now nullable. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset</code> to require the offset. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3de9e361fdd8be7ee83c7946b809b5729d4ef2c4">I3de9e</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Drawers and Sheets to correctly delay presses in case gestures can become scroll events.</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minLines</code> parameter into material and material3 Text, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> which allows setting the minimum height of the component in terms of number of lines (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4af1df6521acaa97edbed5048079b5e81b647dd8">I4af1d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixes an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">pullRefresh</code> was not consuming velocity, causing overscroll to show. Also changed the API signature of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onRelease</code> lambda in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.pullRefresh</code> to return a Float for consumed velocity (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7db6562a865f6ea870a57102f81d04e3d8289c0e">I7db65</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266874741">b/266874741</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code> now expose a progress property indicating the progress between the current (settled) anchor and the closest anchor in the swipe direction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1b31727b4f56df890e336bea9f4de526733aaacc">I1b317</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/271169225">b/271169225</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/276375124">b/276375124</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/276776071">b/276776071</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/270066861">b/270066861</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> dismiss action to appear below the confirm action when the actions stacked over each other to fit into the dialog&#39;s width. This fix aligns the implementation with the Material Design spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I029ded5c6dd79f38b1a060afb3d24dcfb9cf119a">I029de</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235454277">b/235454277</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> will not participate in nested scroll anymore when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">gesturesEnabled</code> is set to false. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I634f33bf0d7e6b4dea5d2225c8e7561b74a42d40">I634f3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/215403277">b/215403277</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> would crash when provided with empty content for slots. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib24a55cf43d4e887f7742691e522d7fc843ce89c">Ib24a5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235588730">b/235588730</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PullRefreshIndicator</code> intercepting clicks/pointer events. (<a href="https://android-review.git.corp.google.com/c/platform/frameworks/support/+/2494256">2494256</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/271777421">b/271777421</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code> would crash in an edge case on orientation change. Layout animations (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.animateContentSize</code>) in/on the sheet content now work smoothly. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2f981d892f163254f0282d6874fb860aae5d0992">I2f981</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266780234">b/266780234</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0-rc01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/81e6706c269471032b283755131d2aa4e8821a89..e423b92ad8e8707ff4031626131f05e33979eac8/compose">Version 1.5.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.5.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.5.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-beta02</h3>

<p>June 7, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d26ca4055c940126ae1663ad0d54aafd23205ea4..df792c9ff86d87f538bab5d7f9dd9f56e2437b15/compose/material">Version 1.5.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.5.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.5.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 24, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68..d26ca4055c940126ae1663ad0d54aafd23205ea4/compose/material">Version 1.5.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawerState</code>&#39;s and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code>&#39;s offset are not nullable anymore. They instead return <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Float.NaN</code> to indicate the absence of the offset. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie98555941822a1609a86926b57a156e671e16778">Ie9855</a>)</li>
<li>Added an option to pass in a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollState</code> when constructing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code> or an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenu</code> for controlling the vertical scroll state of the displayed menu items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb0090cd1b9bb4853e448d82094156a8af39d65b">Idb009</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/185304441">b/185304441</a>)</li>
<li>Add the support for enabling/disabling the gesture of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code> so that user could configure this for more featured bottomsheet (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I40af0ce2206e5967b468c5545324c7a0e9c2e97c">I40af0</a>)</li>
<li>Added a color parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicText</code> to allow efficiently animating or setting text color. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffd88c4c2de7f6922add66b1fc46bdff8853c3f6">Iffd88</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/246961787">b/246961787</a>)</li>
<li>Renaming the Semantics property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isContainer</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isTraversalGroup</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I121f64d7e7be332c41a1fbf10a70ef1ec14ce0dc">I121f6</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> dismiss action to appear below the confirm action when the actions stacked over each other to fit into the dialog&#39;s width. This fix align the implementation with the Material Design spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I029ded5c6dd79f38b1a060afb3d24dcfb9cf119a">I029de</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235454277">b/235454277</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0..6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68/compose/material">Version 1.5.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We are moving the density dependency to the component level. This applies to the following components: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawer</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalDrawer</code>. Please use the new overload provided where density is a parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8fbd8011386bbaa46e3a1492cbaa9766d8f24024">I8fbd8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>April 19, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.5.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597..01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0/compose/material">Version 1.5.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawer</code> internals to use the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableV2</code> APIs. Because of this <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomDrawerState</code> will now only have APIS defined at the class level, it won&#39;t inherit methods/properties from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableState</code>. We&#39;re using composition with an internal <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableV2State</code>. Offset is now a nullable floating point property, the current value and a swipe target value can still be accessed through currentValue and targetValue properties. The previous class level methods such as open/expand/close and properties such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isOpen/isClosed</code> continue to be supported. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad40c08ca8f48afbc451191c788e80584e874b98">Iad40c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/178529942">b/178529942</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/220676296">b/220676296</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated internals of the Switch component. The switch will now preview the closest (target state) when dragging. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id90d466b47eb7eb446ee96e234215f3b0d3e5706">Id90d4</a>)</li>
<li>Animated sheet content (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.animateContentSize</code> on sheet content) in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> has been optimized and now works smoothly. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia913cf9c75949c25a5cc1a6f6dc2b650c95793b9">Ia913c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/270518202">b/270518202</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254446195">b/254446195</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code> will not participate in nested scroll anymore when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">gesturesEnabled</code> is set to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I634f33bf0d7e6b4dea5d2225c8e7561b74a42d40">I634f3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/215403277">b/215403277</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p>April 19, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.2</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5dcb085369a3574f1b09eaaf2a58ee0ea01c22d5..0872f930da585f7fbf6e17c74b1dc42045e8b2c6/compose/material">Version 1.4.2 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p>April 5, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.1</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/c13b30cf6683e0a43585416f30b55e07bf2b560e..5dcb085369a3574f1b09eaaf2a58ee0ea01c22d5/compose/material">Version 1.4.1 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.4.0" data-text="Version 1.4.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ce5f1f96b304c7952d07c5bb472112c4b0ee2312..c5b142d6ab0494c996b2378d5008ac1cd6da75f3/compose/material">Version 1.4.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.3.0</strong></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.minimumInteractiveComponentSize</code>. It can be used to reserve at least 48.dp in size to disambiguate touch interactions if the element would measure smaller. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I33f58e4c11cf74668e97167b91dad26b64ac554b">I33f58</a>, <a href="https://b.corp.google.com/issues/258495559">b/258495559</a>)</li>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalDrawer</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawerState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> has been replaced by the open and close methods and the offset is now nullable. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset</code> to require the offset. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3de9e361fdd8be7ee83c7946b809b5729d4ef2c4">I3de9e</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minLines</code> parameter into material and material3 Text, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> which allows setting the minimum height of the component in terms of number of lines (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4af1df6521acaa97edbed5048079b5e81b647dd8">I4af1d</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minLines</code> parameter to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicText</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTextField</code>. It allows to set the minimum height of these composables in terms of number of lines (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2429479960eef317f467fa054b979c12fd73689d">I24294</a>, <a href="https://b.corp.google.com/issues/122476634">b/122476634</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-rc01</h3>

<p>March 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0-rc01</code> is released with no changes. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522..6022301db806601f282c53b8cbb5a981923a1589/compose/material">Version 1.4.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta02</h3>

<p>February 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677..87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522/compose/material">Version 1.4.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetScaffold</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BottomSheetState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmStateChange</code> param has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmValueChange</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">progress</code> is now exposed as a float value. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> are internal. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expand()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">collapse()</code> instead. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">direction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">overflow</code> have been removed. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">offset</code> has been replaced with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset()</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I323b4ebe42e5a3817f27759749d72ad222ac084b">I323b4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed semantic roles from clickable and selectable surfaces, updated components that used them to set roles using modifier.semantics (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb4ba779b94c5bd69728d09b0318072eef8a6a99">Ibb4ba</a>)</li>
<li>Minor update to the extended Material icons that tweaks the filled <code translate="no" dir="ltr">desktop_mac</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">directions</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">kitchen</code> icons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I65f5e9e1dd6efaa53ebbfc80ac6d8ec923ddb174">I65f5e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta01</h3>

<p>February 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e5dad1e7d1c225f89f7c2d5a39a7a0de8d637d7b..f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677/compose/material">Version 1.4.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixes an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">pullRefresh</code> was not consuming velocity, causing overscroll to show. Also changed the API signature of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onRelease</code> lambda in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.pullRefresh</code> to return a Float for consumed velocity (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7db6562a865f6ea870a57102f81d04e3d8289c0e">I7db65</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266874741">b/266874741</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60dd5ceb7c5703c8ba68f1b7d4a4a883b3f961a8">I60dd5</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>January 11, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/047e199bdcb8a5cd744cc7a2f986631bfb350ec7..adf1c279a86ab3886e1666c08e2c3efba783367b/compose/material">Version 1.4.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IsContainer</code> semantics property on Surfaces. This property will be used in a later change that determines traversal order based on the semantic meaning of elements such as surfaces. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I63379fde102abbee7d5464c50b1c86a59e01e768">I63379</a>)</li>
<li>Mark the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> function in Drawer as non-experimental API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib9c18103d5485a48177a9b57ce40b29656bb4cf1">Ib9c18</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261425368">b/261425368</a>)</li>
<li>Added a track color parameter for circular progress indicators, and a stroke cap parameter for both circular and linear progress indicators. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie668cc47ce9ce3aa688ad3c3ed9e9e15fdbda5e9">Ie668c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/216325962">b/216325962</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222964817">b/222964817</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState.Saver</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberModalBottomSheetState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmStateChange</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">confirmValueChange</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib48d1cbe2671647f5feda1fcde5dee9754c8caa0">Ib48d1</a>)</li>
<li>More return type nullability of deprecated-hidden functions (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf7b0ada56eb08983e6109d30fad5294f6b841f0">Ibf7b0</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.minimumInteractiveComponentSize</code>. It can be used to reserve at least 48.dp in size to disambiguate touch interactions if the element would measure smaller. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I33f58e4c11cf74668e97167b91dad26b64ac554b">I33f58</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/258495559">b/258495559</a>)</li>
<li>Incorporated changes in the Swipeable APIs in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> does not take an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animationSpec</code> parameter anymore and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">offset</code> exposed is now nullable. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requireOffset</code> to require the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">offset</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia2e79162058b143cc40ab6c4b1082126e147a7a2">Ia2e79</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>A <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code>&#39;s sheet now has a maximum width of 640 dp. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I71a4f015f303a2d20c0e8bf5b54ded56533c9701">I71a4f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/234927577">b/234927577</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberPullRefreshState</code> was not updating <code translate="no" dir="ltr">refreshThreshold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">refreshingOffset</code> over time. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifed10d3305317f3a46e7e700ce7759746e1cea0e">Ifed10</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/263159832">b/263159832</a>)</li>
<li>Progress for progress indicators is now properly bounded to its expected range. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a7eb76931af76bac20dbd2879674a60c2899672">I8a7eb</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/262262727">b/262262727</a>)</li>
<li>When <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetState</code> has not received any anchors yet, it will update the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">currentValue</code> without an animation when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateTo</code> are called instead of throwing an exception. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2c91b5c454882c7288425921e13b20ba3a375351">I2c91b</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed the enabled state at the Material 2 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilterChip</code> implementation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id326a2a1749936c585011497bf5bcb3d21a05f9e">Id326a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261329817">b/261329817</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code> would crash if it was <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HalfExpanded</code> when rotating from portrait to landscape. Please ensure you are passing in the correct <code translate="no" dir="ltr">initialValue</code>, for example by checking the configuration. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie8df79fae22ea27329024e0ea3b3f6a240151b87">Ie8df7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/182882364">b/182882364</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code> would crash if the sheet content was empty. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetLayout</code> now allows empty sheet content. If the sheet content is empty, it will only have a Hidden state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2288017e3c5a80a0951cf136064cca5e2fab7cb">Ic2288</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/200980998">b/200980998</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/216693030">b/216693030</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issue</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>When updating from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation:1.4.0-alpha03</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation:1.4.0-alpha04</code>, you might experience a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">java.lang.NoSuchFieldError</code> error. <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/265172081">Here</a> is where the issue was orginially reported. A fix has been submitted, and will be available on the next Compose update. As a work around, update your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material3</code> libraries to the latest version(1.1.0-alpha04) or downgrade your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.foundation</code> to 1.4.0-alpha03.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>October 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.4.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e6ab75d133443eb5c1d92f910f625741041fc591..548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b/compose/material">Version 1.4.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>A new method, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">awaitEachGesture()</code>, for gesture detectors was added. It operates similar to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">forEachGesture()</code>, but the loop over gestures operates entirely within the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AwaitPointerEventScope</code> so events can&#39;t be lost between iterations.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">forEachGesture()</code> has been deprecated in favor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">awaitEachGesture()</code> because it allows events to be lost between gestures. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffc3fb8cf53d0e5eb9b529c023b3e2d29003e86f">Iffc3f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251260206">b/251260206</a>)</li>

<p>No changes since 1.3.0-beta01</p>

<h3 id="1.3.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-beta01</h3>

<p>August 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.3.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/bea814b246f89ff7244e3c6b0648f0b57e47897c..d9910e143f859716fd850a1f0036147622d6089b/compose/material">Version 1.3.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behavior breaking change</strong></p>

<p>Maximum supported elevation in dialogs and popups has been reduced to 8dp.</p>

<p>The maximum supported elevation for Compose dialogs and popups has been reduced from 30dp to 8dp. This change affects both material and ui custom dialogs and popups. This change is made to mitigate an accessibility bug on Android versions below S, and to ensure that accessibility services within those windows are able to interact with the content inside the dialog or popup.</p>

<p>You will only be impacted by this change if you are creating a custom dialog or popup implementation with an elevation set to levels higher than 8dp. Consider lowering the elevation of your dialog or popup. If you need to opt-out from this new behavior, consider forking your own dialog or popup with the desired elevation set. This is not recommended, as accessibility might be negatively impacted and it is on the developer to ensure the bottom part of the dialog or popup is interactable and readable by accessibility services.</p>

<h3 id="1.2.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.2.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-beta01</h3>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.2.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/41a4e31408842caa2b58db5e4ee6ec708464425f..eea19c54f6d94f1c234c4305c1329f7f1427867a/compose/material">Version 1.2.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>This is the first beta release of 1.2!</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldDefaults.BorderStroke</code> composable that draws a border stroke in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldDefaults.BorderBox</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5f295062ff2a3ebc72115df2412062558d226273">I5f295</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>April 20, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.2.0-alpha08</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/7ca43e00a517eaeeedc0a21f482b17f06e3d2181..41a4e31408842caa2b58db5e4ee6ec708464425f/compose/material">Version 1.2.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Partial consumption (down OR position) has been deprecated in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>.  You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">consume()</code> to consume the change completely.  You can use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isConsumed</code> to determine whether or not someone else has previously consumed the change.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange::copy()</code> now always makes a shallow copy. It means that copies of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code> will be consumed once one of the copies is consumed. If you want to create an unbound <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>, use constructor instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie6be471e6ed2a843e38712922c2231fdfd26213a">Ie6be4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/225669674">b/225669674</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>March 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.2.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8..33cb12e8aba043a05b40470a5ef3be1b35114fd5/compose/material">Version 1.2.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyHorizontalGrid</code> are now stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I307c0ce412c7bc762e334e429013c0442bd22fde">I307c0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid/LazyHorizontalGrid</code> and all related apis were moved into .grid subpackage. Please update your imports from androidx.compose.foundation.lazy to androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.grid. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d446e0bed6f27f0394b7dcab1152301e3404b0f">I2d446</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/219942574">b/219942574</a>)</li>
<li>Reverted previous change of relying solely on a View for
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowInsetsControllerCompat</code>, and again require a Window which is
required for managing some window flags. Deprecated
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ViewCompat.getWindowInsetsController</code> in favor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WindowCompat.getInsetsController</code> to ensure that the correct Window is
used (such as if the View is in a dialog). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I660aee32108b59516232b41e05b3f05ae2538554">I660ae</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/219572936">b/219572936</a>)</li>
<li>Text:<code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> is now turned off by default. The
clipping issues as a result of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding=false</code> is handled
and no clipping should occur for tall scripts. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I31c84166ae5241fea3f49e8f293dd9d8a5d712cb">I31c84</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/171394808">b/171394808</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyVerticalGrid</code> API to define cross axis sizes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I17723fdc6302a345dd643fb637e1644168a2a321">I17723</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>February 23, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.2.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/db2ecbef194afcddfaede22e1d884a8959a9277c..9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8/compose/material">Version 1.2.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Add support for filter chips</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I39a6e25725a71191a2e78c2162419935d487ac59">I39a6e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/192585545">b/192585545</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextFieldDecorationBox</code> and
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextFieldDecorationBox</code>. Using them together with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTextField</code>
will help you build custom text field based on Material Design text
fields but with more options for customisation.</li>
<li>Provided a way to adjust horizontal and vertical paddings in text fields. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c9f168a687e337670c266e1eb3e985da6aebdc3">I8c9f1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/203764564">b/203764564</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/191543915">b/191543915</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/189971673">b/189971673</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/183136600">b/183136600</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179882597">b/179882597</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/168003617">b/168003617</a>)</li>
<li><p>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTarget</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTargetMarker</code> and
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableOpenTarget</code> that allows compile time reporting of when
a composable function is called targeting an applier it was not
designed to use.</p>

<p>In most cases the  annotations can be inferred by the compose
compiler plugin so using these annotation directly should be
rare . The cases that cannot be inferred include creating and
using a custom applier, abstract composable functions (such as
interface methods), fields or global variables that are
composable lambdas (local variables and parameters are inferred),
or when using  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeNode</code> or a related composable functions.</p>

<p>For custom appliers the composable functions that calls
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeNode</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ReusableComposeNode</code> need to add a
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompoableTarget</code> annotation for the function and any
composable lambda parameter types. It is recommended, however,
to create an annotation that is annotated with
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTargetMarker</code> and then the  marked annotation be used
instead of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTarget</code> directly. A composable annotation
marked with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTargetMarker</code> is equivalent to a
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposbleTarget</code> with the fully qualified name of the attribute
class as the applier parameter. For an example of using
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposableTargetMarker</code> see <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anroidx.compose.ui.UiComposable</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38f11b789291db89fc0bb92fc14ac5b3fcba0283">I38f11</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>January 26, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.2.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f09f3e0f47cacc65a631115deac08ee8cc132ceb..9dceceb54300ed028a7e8fc7a3454f270337ffde/compose/material">Version 1.2.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NonRestartableComposable</code> to methods that are overloads
of existing methods without complex logic. This reduces compiler
generated memoization checks (equals) for all parameters which
are repeated in the inner function that is called. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I90490b1a28bada20840ab59e47245c00c6253d11">I90490</a>)</li>
<li>Add support for action chip (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I07100d433428017c69701aa0dd6a1490e4ea3522">I07100</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/192585545">b/192585545</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.1.0" data-text="Version 1.1.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0</h3>

<p>February 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.1.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/0310f2e9c177573a16c2d594fffabaada9b446ea..f9e9589a03c4b53f4401cc0cb8f763526fb885c7/compose/material">Version 1.1.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.0.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Stable support for the Android 12 <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/c/platform/frameworks/support/+/1795727/">Overscroll effect</a></li>
<li>Improvements to touch target sizing</li>
<li>Note that, with respect to Compose 1.0, Material components will expand their layout space to meet Material <a href="https://material.io/design/usability/accessibility.html">accessibility guidelines</a> for <a href="https://material.io/design/usability/accessibility.html#layout-and-typography">touch target size</a>. For instance, Button touch target will expand to a minimum size of 48x48dp, even if you set the Button&#39;s size to be smaller. This aligns Compose Material to the same behavior of Material Design Components, providing consistent behavior if you mix Views and Compose. This change also ensures that when you create your UI using Compose Material components, minimum requirements for touch target accessibility will be met.</li>
<li>Stable Support for <a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/material3/package-summary#navigationrail">Navigation Rail</a></li>
<li>Graduates a number of previously experimental APIs to stable</li>
<li><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-kotlin">Support</a> for newer versions of Kotlin</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-rc03" data-text="Version 1.1.0-rc03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-rc03</h3>

<p>January 26, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.1.0-rc03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/8b1e748d80de10c087ce57eaaa93cd209cccebad..0310f2e9c177573a16c2d594fffabaada9b446ea/compose/material">Version 1.1.0-rc03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Behaviour Changes</strong></p>

<p>Note that, with respect to Compose 1.0, Material components will expand their layout space to meet Material <a href="https://material.io/design/usability/accessibility.html">accessibility guidelines</a> <a href="https://material.io/design/usability/accessibility.html#layout-and-typography">touch target</a> size. For instance, Button touch target will expand to a minimum size of 48x48dp, even if you set the Button&#39;s size to be smaller. This aligns Compose Material to the same behavior of Material Design Components, providing consistent behavior if you mix Views and Compose. This change also ensures that when you create your UI using Compose Material components, minimum requirements for touch target accessibility will be met.</p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added some better debug information for the layout inspector when inspecting minimum touch target modifiers.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/c/platform/frameworks/support/+/1955036/">aosp/1955036</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>October 13, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.1.0-alpha06</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/da9716386798fc4e39075f54e5bd3317384a63e6..db0888af4fa9a8eaeaf55cc1f120724bc67bdb20/compose/material">Version 1.1.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>A child-less overload for Layout was added, with improved efficiency (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib0d9a0f11936c0568d20e26a3c6eaa3f938e0ccd">Ib0d9a</a>)</li>
<li>Implementation of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenu</code> based on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExposedDropdownMenuBox</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownMenu</code> inside (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If60b2e6c7c139d4d4c134c714e2803f531a6c72a">If60b2</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">dismissOnOutsideClick</code> was added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PopupProperties</code>, replacing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dismissOnClickOutside</code> which was deprecated. The new property receives the click position and the anchor bounds, providing finer control over whether onDismissRequest should be invoked or not. For example, this can be useful to prevent anchor dismissal for touches on the anchor.
<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">updateAndroidWindowManagerFlags</code> was added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PopupProperties</code>, offering low-level control over the flags passed by the popup to the Android WindowManager. The parameter of the lambda will be the flags calculated from the PopupProperties values that result in WindowManager flags: e.g. focusable. The result of the lambda will be the final flags which will be passed to the Android WindowManager. By default, updateAndroidWindowManagerFlags will leave the flags calculated from parameters unchanged. This API should be used with caution, only in cases where the popup has very specific behavior requirements. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6e9f9d393dc12bd1ea7ae294af1761817f154735">I6e9f9</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>September 29, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material:material-*:1.1.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1a3dcfb231517d6104969f17063fcc6c97ba6eeb..da9716386798fc4e39075f54e5bd3317384a63e6/compose/material">Version 1.1.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Adds minimum touch target sizing for Material components that do not have an accessible touch target. As this adds extra spacing around components to make sure they have a large enough touch target, this may change existing UIs that assume the size of these components is their visual size, and doesn&#39;t account for touch target size. You can use the experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalMinimumTouchTargetEnforcement</code> composition local to disable this behavior across a hierarchy, but this is intended only to be a temporary escape hatch while updating existing UIs to account for the new minimum size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9b966a79a290538d8d450aa732b5092760cbece4">I9b966</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/149691127">b/149691127</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/171509422">b/171509422</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental TextFieldColorsWithIcons interface, extending TextFieldColors to provide InteractionSource to the leadingColor and trailingColor. This enables modifying the appearance of TextField according to the focus state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6692391098f7840a491bd175da2dfde116718bbc">I66923</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/198402662">b/198402662</a>)</li>
</ul>

respect <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dp.Hairline</code> for the thickness parameter
